  void execute(int separator, int text, int templateds)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int C2 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;

    int temporaryText = 0;

    lessPreciseBound((R < (((((((((((8 * text) * templateds) + ((8 * separator) * templateds)) + ((8 * separator) * text)) + ((8 * text) * text)) + ((8 * separator) * separator)) + ((8 * templateds) * templateds)) + (8 * text)) + (8 * templateds)) + (8 * separator)) + 8)) || (R == (((((((((((8 * text) * templateds) + ((8 * separator) * templateds)) + ((8 * separator) * text)) + ((8 * text) * text)) + ((8 * separator) * separator)) + ((8 * templateds) * templateds)) + (8 * text)) + (8 * templateds)) + (8 * separator)) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < ((text * templateds) + (separator * templateds))) || (R == ((text * templateds) + (separator * templateds))));
    if ((((text < 1) || (text == 1)) || ((templateds < 0) || (templateds == 0))) || ((separator < 0) || (separator == 0)))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    int i = 0;
    while (i < templateds)
    {
      int j = 0;

        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;

abstract class TemplateEngineMultiTrace  {
  void execute(int text, int choice)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    int temporaryText = 0;
    int lastIndexOfText = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < ((8 * text) + 8)) || (R == ((8 * text) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < text) || (R == text));
    if ((text < 1) || (text == 1))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    if (!((choice < 10)) && !((choice == 10)))
    {
      int i = 0;
      while (i < text)
      {
        {
          temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
          chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
          lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
        }
        D1p = D1; D1 = 0; C1 = C1 + 1;D1 = D1 + chunk;
        R = R + chunk;
        i = i + 1;
      }
    }
    else
    {
      int j = 0;
      while (j < text)
      {
        {
          temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
          chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
          lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
        }
        D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + chunk;
        R = R + chunk;
        j = j + 1;
      }
    }
  }

  public abstract void lessPreciseBound(boolean assertion);

abstract class TemplateEngineSimplifiedVariant  {
  void execute(int text)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;

    int temporaryText = 0;
    int lastIndexOfText = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < (((8 * text) + (text * 8)) + 8)) || (R == (((8 * text) + (text * 8)) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < (text + text)) || (R == (text + text)));
    if ((text < 1) || (text == 1))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    int i = 0;
    while (i < text)
    {
      {
        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
      }
      D1p = D1; D1 = 0; C1 = C1 + 1;D1 = D1 + chunk;
      R = R + chunk;
      D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + 1;
      R = R + 1;
      i = i + 1;
    }
  }

abstract class Modify  {
  void execute(int str)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < ((8 * str) + 8)) || (R == ((8 * str) + 8)));
    mostPreciseBound((R < str) || (R == str));
    if ((str < 0) || (str == 0))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int buffer = 0;
    int i = 0;
    while (i < str)

abstract class Replace  {
  void execute(int replacement, int text, int searchString, int max)
  {
    int C0 = 0;
    int C1 = 0;
    int D0 = 0;
    int D0p = 0;
    int D1 = 0;
    int D1p = 0;
    int BOOLEAN_SEPARATOR = 10;
    int R = 0;
    int temporaryText = 0;
    int lastIndexOfText = 0;
    lessPreciseBound((R < ((8 + (8 * text)) + ((8 * text) * replacement))) || (R == ((8 + (8 * text)) + ((8 * text) * replacement))));
    mostPreciseBound((R < (text + (text * replacement))) || (R == (text + (text * replacement))));
    if (((((text < 1) || (text == 1)) || ((searchString < 0) || (searchString == 0))) || ((max < 0) || (max == 0))) || ((replacement < 0) || (replacement == 0)))
    {
      return;
    }
    else
    {
      ;
    }
    int chunk = 0;
    int i = 0;
    while ((i + 1) < text)
    {
      {
        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
      }
      D0p = D0; D0 = 0; C0 = C0 + 1;D0 = D0 + chunk;
      R = R + chunk;
      D1p = D1; D1 = 0; C1 = C1 + 1;D1 = D1 + replacement;
      R = R + replacement;
      {
        temporaryText = ndInt2(lastIndexOfText, text);
        chunk = temporaryText - lastIndexOfText;
        lastIndexOfText = temporaryText;
      }
      i = i + 2;
    }
  }

  // Keep in sync with brbo2
